Weather Report 165

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the Yangtze River basin is cloudy with thunderstorms and occasional heavy fog due to a low pressure system in Jiangxi moving northeast and east. There is a cyclone in this area and the East China Sea, and the wind is picking up along the Shandong coast and is unpredictable. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 59.7 degrees and the lowest was 45.5 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 44.8 degrees and the lowest was 36.0 degrees.

Letters to the Editor 166

Sir, I am writing on behalf of my client, Mr. Hu Tiaoyi, who was surprised to read in the news column of the Shen Bao on the 1st of this month a report entitled "Hu Zhaoxi Dies for His Wife". Although I once tried to mediate the rift between Hu Zhaoxi and his wife, there were many relatives and friends besides the lawyers on both sides who knew about the matter. Later, because the mediation was ineffective, each side went to extremes, and the mediator was helpless. The matter was then resolved by agreement between the lawyers on both sides. The facts are all there, and it is impossible to point fingers at random. I am now writing this letter on behalf of my client to ask your newspaper to correct the report based on the facts for the public to see. Yours sincerely, Lawyer Chen Zhongyin, February 3rd.

Sir, I have read in your local news column of February 2 the article "New Combination of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Hubei Guilds in the Chinese Medicine Industry", which states, "The regular expenses are borne by the industry, divided into two types: A, those who establish their own shops pay 40 yuan at a time; B, those who are affiliated with a firm pay 20 yuan at a time." This kind of regulation is the start-up fee that our members have agreed to share, and it must be approved by the higher-level guild before it can be collected. Because it is slightly inconsistent with the facts, I am afraid it will cause misunderstandings. Therefore, I am writing this letter to ask you to examine and publish it in the letters to the editor column to correct it. I would be grateful if you could do so. Yours sincerely, Sichuan, Yunnan, and Hubei Group Office, Shanghai Chinese Medicine Industry Guild. Sir, I have read the article "New Combination of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Hubei Guilds in the Chinese Medicine Industry" in your local news section of February 2, which is not entirely correct. On the 25th of this month, the Sichuan, Yunnan, and Hubei Group held a meeting to establish the group. Our association sent Executive Committee member Chen Wenming to attend and provide guidance. According to Chen's report, the organization of the group did not comply with the group rules drafted by our association and arbitrarily imposed membership fees, which was illegal. Chen stated his objection at the meeting. The group then submitted a report to the association, and the 11th Executive Committee meeting of our association decided that the crude organization of the group was difficult to record. In addition to notifying the group to reorganize according to law and returning the original documents, a special letter was sent to clarify the matter. Please allow it to be published in the letters to the editor column to show the facts. Thank you very much for your public assistance. Yours sincerely, Executive Committee, Shanghai Chinese Medicine Industry Guild, February 3rd.

Sir, I have read today's news in your newspaper about the French Concession Court continuing to hear the case of the Day and Night Bank, which states that "the five places belonging to the Gongfa Company, including the Hot Spring Bathhouse, Jiufu Company, and Chinese and Western Pharmacy", etc., are not true. Our company is a limited company and was registered with the National Registration Bureau in the 17th year of the Republic of China in accordance with the law, holding Registration No. 205. It has nothing to do with Gongfa Company. I am sincerely afraid that all circles will misunderstand. Therefore, I am writing this letter to clarify the matter and hope that you will publish it in the letters to the editor column to correct it to clarify the truth. To build public amity, Yours sincerely, Jiufu Co., Ltd., February 3rd.

Educational News Highlights

Opening of the Shandong Provincial Educational Administrative Conference 167

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Department of Education convened the presidents of provincial schools to hold the second provincial educational administrative conference. The preparations have been reported in previous news. Yesterday (the 1st) at 10:00 a.m., the opening ceremony was held at the Provincial Women's Normal School in Nanguan. All members and staff except Sun Yuxi, the president of the Second Middle School, and Li Taihua, the president of the Third Middle School, were present. The only guests were Yang Zhensheng, the president of the National Qingdao University. The Jinan branch of the Commercial Press and the World Book Company came to the meeting to distribute educational supplies for entertainment. At 10:00 a.m., the meeting was held as scheduled. The chairman was He Siyuan, the master of ceremonies was Liu Cixiao, and the recorder was Yang Peng. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, saying that today is the opening of the second educational administrative conference. The most important task is to discuss the administrative difficulties of the 19th year and seek a solution for removal and improvement. At the first meeting last year, the difficulties of the 18th year were discussed, and a solution for removal and improvement was requested. However, after a year of implementation, many difficulties have arisen. This time, we must discuss the materials based on experience and earnestly remove and improve them. The scope of this discussion can be summarized as follows: (1) Difficulties: problems regarding the salary clock allocation of teachers and staff, and the distribution of temporary fees must be discussed. The most important problem is to pay attention to the detailed and rapid creation of budgets to avoid repeated approvals, corrections, and early arrival and early issuance regarding the problem of recruiting students, such as the enrollment of the Sixth Middle School and the First Middle School. Up to 1,000 applicants are there. The enrollment of one teacher is 40, and there are as many as 700 applicants. This is a good phenomenon, but it is enough to prove that the supply of schools does not meet the demand. We should discuss how to accommodate students or expand classes regarding equipment problems. We should discuss the methods of equipment for the convenience of students' studies, books, instruments, and all other equipment. Last month, Japanese supervisors came to Jinan to visit education and were surprised by the good atmosphere of the youth, but they were dissatisfied with the imperfection of the equipment. This is limited by financial resources, but it must also be discussed in detail to the extent of financial resources. Regarding the problem of enrollment, the Ministry of Education ordered that students from unregistered private schools should not be recruited. There have been many disputes in the past, and this should also be discussed. (2) Budget issues: In the 18th year, there were 20,020 primary and secondary schools in the province, with 700,000 students. The 19th year is not over, and it is estimated that there will be at least 35,000 primary and secondary schools up and down, with 1 million students. The education expenditure in the 18th year was 2.2 million yuan, and in the 19th year it was 2.8 million yuan. In the 20th year, the number of schools and students will increase, and the treatment of teachers and staff will be improved, so the budget will naturally have to increase. It is estimated that it can be increased to 3 million yuan. This budget should be discussed on how to distribute it and must be submitted to the central government by March 1 at the latest. (3) The entire education plan of the province: In order to accommodate as many students as possible, in addition to increasing classes in the original schools, it is planned to expand various schools throughout the province. To sum up in one sentence, the scope of discussion of this meeting is (1) to solve difficulties, (2) to prepare the 20th-year budget, and (3) to create the whole plan. The meeting method is different from the previous one. This time, a round table is adopted, so that each school can submit proposals as much as possible, without limiting the form, time, and scope. Also, the proposals of the previous general meeting must first be reviewed by the review committee, and the power of approval seems to be in the hands of the review committee. This time, the review committee will be changed to a research nature, and the results of the research will be submitted to the general meeting for public decision. Next, the guests Yang Zhensheng, Zhou Chao, the president of the Third Normal School, Sun Wei Yue, the president of the First Middle School, and Zhu Jingtang, the president of the Second Vocational School, spoke. Finally, Yang Chengrong, the director of the Shandong Mass Education Museum, reported on the work of the museum. At this point, the chairman announced that from tomorrow onwards, two formal meetings will be held every day from 9:00 a.m. to 2:00 p.m., and the meeting period is uncertain, depending on the number of proposals. The ceremony was completed, and the meeting was adjourned. After the meeting, a dinner was held in the school.

The Ministry of Education Orders Mongolian and Tibetan Banners and Sects to Send Outstanding Students to Normal Schools in the Interior 168

The Ministry of Education, in order to develop Mongolian and Tibetan education and train primary school teachers, yesterday issued an order to the Mongolian and Tibetan banners and sects to select outstanding and qualified students to study in normal high schools, normal science departments, or rural teachers' schools in the interior or border provinces to train teachers to return to their hometowns to serve. It is said that the number of schools set up in Mongolian and Tibetan areas is small. Although there are various reasons, the lack of teachers is one of the main reasons. In order to popularize Mongolian and Tibetan education, training teachers is an urgent task today. The Ministry has seen this and, in addition to actively preparing Mongolian and Tibetan schools in Nanjing and Xikang to set up normal classes and train such talents, the normal schools in the interior or border provinces that have achieved success can also train excellent teachers for Mongolian and Tibetan areas. For this reason, the Ministry orders each banner and sect to quickly select outstanding and qualified young students to study in normal schools, normal high school science departments, and rural normal schools in the interior or border provinces to train suitable teachers to return to their hometowns and engage in local education work. This is very important. This order.

Local News

Party and Government Agencies Investigate the Zhonggong School Incident 171

The Board of Directors Telegraphs the Ministry of Education for Handling

(Kuomintang News Agency) The sudden change in the Zhonggong School turmoil was reported yesterday. However, the content of the school is complex and changes rapidly. It is specially reported separately.

▲ The Board of Directors telegraphed the Ministry of Education. After the drastic change in the school the day before yesterday (2nd), Chairman Cai immediately convened a temporary meeting of the Board of Directors to seek a solution. It was originally scheduled to be held at Cai's residence at 6:00 p.m. However, seeing Ma Junwu instigating three student representatives to come to the scene to disrupt the meeting, the location was temporarily changed to the Cangzhou Hotel. A total of seven directors arrived at the Cangzhou Hotel: Cai Yuanpei, Gao Yihan, Wang Yunwu, Liu Binglin, Yang Xingfo, Ding Gouyin, and Ma Junwu. As they were about to start the meeting, the three disrupting students rushed to the scene again. All the directors were very dissatisfied. Therefore, a general resignation was proposed. It is now heard that Chairman Cai has telegraphed the details to the Ministry of Education and stated that the directors cannot be held responsible. The Ministry of Education is asked to handle everything.

▲ Party and government agencies sent personnel to investigate. After the representatives the day before yesterday aroused the public anger of all students and resisted in self-defense, the students closed all the offices and sent classmates to guard the doors of each office to prevent the representatives from returning to the school to take control under false pretenses. Yesterday afternoon, personnel from the Municipal Party Department, the Government Public Security Bureau, and the Municipal Education Bureau came to the school with Battalion Commander Xiong and District Chief Yang to inspect the school for a week. They thought the situation was very good and instructed the students not to disturb each other and to wait quietly for the Ministry of Education to issue a clear order to solve the problem. It is also heard that Chen, the Vice Minister of the Ministry of Education, happened to come to Shanghai on official business at the time of the Zhonggong School turmoil. He has a clear understanding of the truth of the school turmoil. He returned to Beijing yesterday, and it is expected that a thorough solution will be announced soon.

▲ Ma Junwu's enticement of Battalion Commander Xiong. According to a source from a certain agency, when the school was being assaulted the day before yesterday, Ma Junwu asked the battalion headquarters to send a team to suppress the incident and offered a letter of appointment, asking Battalion Commander Xiong to serve as a military instructor with a monthly salary of 200 yuan. Battalion Commander Xiong considered it an insult and strongly rejected it. Later, the battalion headquarters received a phone call from the Public Security Bureau, and Battalion Commander Xiong sent a company of soldiers to maintain order.

▲ The students issued a statement to the faculty. The students of the school sent a letter to the faculty yesterday, stating that Mr. Ma Junwu had been approved to resign by the Board of Directors and had long lost his qualifications as president. All the letters of appointment and all documents issued recently in the name of the president would not have any effect. Teachers are intelligent and should not be fooled.

▲ The announcement of the extension of the Zhonggong New Students. The first enrollment examination for new students for the winter vacation was originally scheduled to be announced on the 4th, but it could not be announced as scheduled due to unforeseen circumstances. It is heard that it is planned to publish a notice in the newspaper announcing the date of the announcement and to notify the admitted students one by one.

▲ The attitude of the current faculty members. The current faculty members of Zhonggong School, Pan Guangdan and others, cannot use the name of Zhonggong faculty members because the contracts of the previous faculty members have expired. Moreover, the executive committee of the current faculty members was elected at the Zhongshe in Weihaiwei Road the day before yesterday. To avoid confusing the public, it is planned to publish a notice to make a solemn statement.

Dr. Wang Jingqi Discusses the Key Problems of Labor Education 173

▲ There are special difficulties in addition to the difficulties of ordinary education.

Dr. Wang Jingqi, the president of the National Labor University, recently published his opinions on labor education due to numerous inquiries about the situation. The general gist is as follows:

I have only been at Labor University for a few weeks. I have not yet studied the situation thoroughly, so I cannot talk about improvements. However, if I just follow my personal behavior, it is very simple. I just need to earnestly do every word of the oath I took on the 19th of last month. What I said to the portrait of the late Premier was the truth. I should also do real things for the school. Before various parties advised me to take on the role of Labor University president, a few friends advised me not to, saying, "Running an educational institution is the most difficult thing, and running a Labor University is the most difficult among the difficult." Therefore, some still advocated that I should go abroad or handle diplomacy domestically, and not engage in educational administration because I have little experience or confidence in this area. However, after seeking consent, I never declined or retreated from difficulties. But today, I also feel that in addition to the difficulties of running things in the ordinary education field, the Labor University has two special difficulties.

One is the special understanding of labor education in our country, namely, the so-called "labor educationization" and "education laborization." This is the ideal advocated and implemented by the Kuomintang after unifying China. This most noble ideal involves transferring the most profound knowledge (universities) to the lowest level of society. In developed countries in Europe and America, as far as I know, it is still in the realm of ideals. What they call labor education can be summarized into two types:

First, vocational schools provide practical and necessary skills to society, giving people the opportunity to study and work part-time. Of course, the level of knowledge cannot keep up with that of students at other universities.

Second, the state and society find ways to enable poor children to study advanced knowledge in universities.

The Labor University-ization and university laborization ideals in our country are at a higher level than those of other countries, making laborers receive university education or making those receiving university education engage in labor at the same time. In addition to the ordinary university system, a period of work experimentation is added. The first question is whether the workers have interest in it and whether they can allocate time and ability properly.

The second is the problem of the Labor University factory. The Labor University factory was originally a model factory. In the early years, it lost money every year. After several years, not only did it not have sufficient power to develop, but it also declined. Furthermore, whether its equipment is suitable for students to work with is also a problem. All industries operated by the state, no matter what country or how well managed, are inferior to those operated by merchants. Therefore, state-owned factories have always lost money, especially in China. It is impossible for the Labor University factory to be entirely operated by students without workers. Even if students do only a part of the work, the cost of raw materials, the time consumption, and the impact on the progress of the workers are extremely inconvenient. Assuming that the current Labor University factory is still operated by the school and students are added for practice, it will inevitably lose money, but there is no money to lose. If the factory is closed down, the machinery will not be easily preserved. If it is not closed down, where does the school have so many financial resources to subsidize it? If it is not closed down and it is allowed to circulate and take on more external orders, where will the circulating capital for manufacturing goods come from? These points are unavoidable difficulties for the Labor University in running a factory. What I am specially pointing out is not that I am afraid to move forward, but that I want the people of society to know the key problems of the Labor University so that they can provide enlightened opinions at any time. I know it is difficult, but I am still willing to do it, and there is no strange method. However, the first step is how to find ways to save costs and concentrate financial resources to reorganize, and I hope that the government will provide monthly financial assistance, so that I can save. The Labor University has not been established for long, and it has suffered many difficulties. Its vitality has not yet been fully restored. I only hope that the students and colleagues in the school can work together to promote the unprecedented labor education in China and lead people to a bright and upright path. Abiding by the oath of January 19th would be a blessing for my entire life.

The editorial and survey matters were handed over to the editorial committee and survey committee respectively for handling. Committee member Wu Kaixian was responsible for raising the funds. Automotive News Special

Citroen's Planned New Car for Sale at a Particularly Low Price 179

Citroen cars are famous throughout the world for their excellent structure and reliable quality, which has been the case for many years. Furthermore, their low selling price is unmatched in the automotive industry. In 1926, the company added a large manufacturing plant in the Four Roads area of ​​Bourgogne, using the latest scientific methods to manufacture large quantities of vehicles to meet the needs of all parts of the world. Today, the organization of the factory is becoming more and more perfect, and the products are becoming more and more refined. The new cars planned by them are also improving with each passing day. I will briefly describe what I know as follows.

The most important new car planned by the factory is a four-cylinder sedan with a total selling price of only 185 pounds. Based on the absolute reliability of the currently popular 13-36 horsepower four-cylinder Citroen chassis, you can imagine the excellence and beauty of the new car, as its construction is similar. The new car is given the beautiful name of "Gelton." The body structure is extremely excellent, extremely beautiful, and its spaciousness and comfort are even more unattainable. The car has four doors and six windows. All the equipment that car enthusiasts are accustomed to is available. For those who like to use eight active roofs, safety glass, bumpers, and luggage racks, there is the Kalalantong style to meet their needs. The selling price of the new car with these accessories is only 215 pounds. As for the six-seater family-style new car, the selling price is 210 pounds.

As for the six-cylinder models, there is the Bourgogne sedan, specially priced at 235 pounds. The one equipped with active roof equipment is called the "Bourg Kailai" style. The seven-seater sells for 260 pounds.

A Study of Automobile Driving and Color by Pei Gan 180

▲ The use of color is related to safety

▲ More attention should be paid to driving a car

At first glance, the issue of color and car safety seems to be unrelated. However, because color has a very strong reflective power, it is closely related to the safety of driving. Traffic experts widely use color for various things, from children to trucks. They know that the reflected light of color can be clearly felt even at long distances, at dusk, or after dark, as if it were daytime.

The Safety Department of the American Automobile Association recently published its research results, stating that children on the street wearing light-colored clothes are more noticeable at a distance than those wearing dark-colored clothes. Therefore, children should not be allowed to pass through the main roads unless they are extremely cautious, and car drivers must be warned from a distance due to the light reflected by light-colored clothing.

Color is also very important in avoiding accidents on the road. The method is to use various signs and symbols to draw attention to them. The principle is that some colors have the special quality of reflecting light, so people can recognize various signs, objects, and symbols at a glance.

The stronger the reflection of color, the easier it is to spot it at a distance, and it can attract attention even in dimly lit places. Therefore, the Road Safety Department has put a lot of effort into this research. According to color experts, white has the strongest reflective power among all colors, followed by cream. After that, in descending order, are ivory, leather tan, light green, yellow, gray, light blue, light red, dark brown, dark red, and dark green.

From the above, we know that white is the best color on the road. If used with black, whether as text or as a background, its reflective power is even stronger due to contrast. Therefore, black and white are often used together as signs and symbols. The adoption of other colors sometimes has an unusual reflective power because the use of incompatible colors together can often attract attention, exceeding both black and white. The Road Marking Committee of the American Society of Mechanical Engineers has

The Manifestation of Gender Equality in Turkey by Ji Ren 181

Turkey is known as a "man's country" because of its emphasis on men and its disregard for women. In recent years, the women's rights movement has been very popular in various countries, and Turkey has also responded. A woman in Constantine is currently studying car driving, passed the examination by the Engineering Bureau, and was given a chauffeur's license to drive a taxi.

The lady's name is Ma Meihai, a beautiful 29-year-old who entered a car school. She is physically fit and has special achievements. For this test, the lady chose a new Chevrolet sedan, equipped with a business trip accessory. The test results were satisfactory. Today, the lady is driving passengers between cities, making her the first female driver in the country.

Page 18

After investigating the national motorcycle transportation situation, they established a unified road transportation agreement. The commonly used color combinations they cited are as follows: railroad crossings, white background with black text; railroad crossing entrances, yellow background with black text; stop, yellow background with red text; slow down, yellow background with black text; caution, black text on yellow background; winding one-way, white arrow on black background; inquiry, white background with black text; no parking, white background with red text; limited parking, white background with green text; pedestrian restrictions, white background with blue text; other restrictions, white background with black text.

The use of colors other than black and white together is considered by car drivers or pedestrians to be a special warning that requires their attention. From a psychological point of view, anything that disturbs the driver outside of normal routines is not appropriate. However, the various colors listed above, whether background or text, are rich in reflected light. Is black text on a white background or white text on a black background better? This question should be determined based on whether or not lights need to be used for illumination at night. If lights need to be used, then a black background with white text is best. In general, a black background is good at absorbing light and making the white text more obvious.

Therefore, from the perspective of the safety of car drivers, white is an important color. Therefore, ground markings, fences, pillars, tree trunks, etc. are mostly painted white, which can have a strong reflection even on rainy and foggy days. Fences painted white can also reduce danger in winding places. White markings on the road also have a huge effect. The most common marking on the road is the center line, which is often marked in white. In the past, road engineers did not know that white had a strong reflective power, so they used black lines as boundaries.

The American Society of Mechanical Engineers also has regulations for the materials used for marking. All materials such as wood and metal are detailed. The type of paint also has a certain standard. Metal signs and symbols must be coated with enamel-like oil paint for durability. The paint composition of wooden signs must be non-changing and non-fading, and the surface must be smooth, durable, and free of cracks. When making wooden signs, the paint must be applied three times to prevent color loss. Each time it is applied, it must be allowed to dry before applying more. If fences and pillars are painted in this way, and the paint is of high quality, their lifespan can be extended for three years.

Drivers of trucks often use a wooden fake hand to signal to cars behind them when turning left or right. This wooden hand is often painted white for easy viewing. The reflected light of white also has other convenient uses that are used by individual car drivers. For example, when driving into a garage at night and feeling dark and inconvenient, you can draw two white lines on the narrow road in advance for the wheels to follow when moving, and draw a white line inside the garage as a stop mark, which is extremely safe.

New Information on Zhejiang Province Highways 182

The most developed construction project in Zhejiang Province is highways. Since Director Chen took office, he has been carrying out the project step by step. The six major trunk lines can be completed one after another, which is of no small benefit to facilitating transportation and benefiting the people. The situation of each line is recorded as follows:

1. The Hangzhou-Changxing Line runs from Hangzhou to Changxing's Fuzi Mountain, with a branch line from Wukang to Mogan Mountain. This line goes directly to the capital. Currently, the line is delayed because of gravel piles on the Jiangsu road in Yixing.

2. The Xiaoshao Line runs from Xixing Riverside to Shaoxian's Wuyunmen, connecting the privately-run Shengxin Yu road line.

3. The Hangping Line runs from Hangzhou to Pinghu, passing through Changan, Haining, and Dazha Pu. Recently, the road surface construction of the Zha Ping section has not been completed, and it cannot be opened to traffic for a while. There is also the Yuanhua Town branch line. This line can be connected to the Jiangsu road to reach Shanghai.

4. The Hangchang Line has now been opened to Yuqian Changhua. Because the bridge there has not been completed and construction is difficult, it can be opened to traffic to reach Anhui Province once it is completed. However, this line passes through the Hangzhou-Yu's Lin Liang privately-run automobile companies.

5. The Hangfu Line, from Hangzhou directly to Fuyang, is the shortest line. It is privately-run and has not been perfected. The Highway Bureau has taken it back and allocated 130,000 yuan to actively repair it. It will be opened to traffic in the spring tea

Overseas News

World's Automotive Rare News Pei Gan 185

▲ French automobile industry develops The French automobile manufacturing industry has developed very well recently. Compared with all countries in the world, the United States is the champion, followed by France. Compared with the various industries in France, the automobile manufacturing industry ranks third. The first is wheat production, and the second is the wine industry. Although American-made, British-made, and German-made cars are often exported to France, according to statistics, for every two foreign cars shipped to France, France will exceed it by exporting five cars. Therefore, no matter what, its automobile export industry will certainly exceed imports by far. The French government levies particularly high import taxes on automobiles. For cars with more than 15 horsepower, whether they are assembled in France or imported as complete vehicles from foreign countries, a very high tariff must be levied. In comparison, Citroen Renault and other cars manufactured in France with no more than 10 horsepower have many advantages. The national wealth occupied by the French automobile industry is 6,500,000,000 francs, the wheat industry is 11 billion francs, the wine industry is 7 billion francs, and the silk industry is 6 billion francs. The steel used by France to manufacture cars last year was enough to build 25 large iron towers with surplus. A total of 245,000 tons of steel, 45,000 tons of cast iron, 12,000 tons of copper, 4,500 tons of paint, 3,300 tons of cotton, and 250,000 square meters of glass were used, which is also very impressive.

▲ Self-driving rental cars The Hanless Company in Camden Town, England, has recently created a new self-driving rental car business. The company prepares six-cylinder and eight-cylinder Studebaker cars. There are no drivers, and the renters drive themselves. The fee is 11 pence per mile, one shilling, or one shilling and three pence, etc., depending on the newness and size of the car. A reduction of one or two pence will be given after using more than 50 miles. From then on, similar deductions will be made. There are other preferential discounts for renters who use the car for a certain distance and shorten the time during the year. This method is very convenient for foreign tourists because they can get suitable transportation even if their stay is limited. Those who like to drive but do not want to buy a car are also very welcome to this rental method.

▲ Feixia Cars Win Honors Repeatedly In addition to driving speed, automobile competitions include various competitions such as the beauty of the car body and the comfort of driving. In this regard, Feixia cars often win in European competitions. (1) In the Sadu Pei competition in Portugal, the Feixia No. 525 four-wheeled van won. In the Calia local competition, the Feixia two-seater No. 521 car won the first prize. (2) In the Salando competition in Italy, Feixia cars of various types won the first prize. (3) In France, in the Leli local competition, Feixia cars won the standard first prize among cars manufactured in foreign countries.

▲ Marius cars sell for 100 pounds Marius small cars have always been known for their exquisiteness and durability. Sir William Marius, the owner, decided to sell them to the public for 100 pounds. This plan has been realized. The Marius car factory has sold the Marius small car with two seats for 100 gold pounds thanks to its large output and special economic manufacturing methods. This new car is slightly different from the ordinary Marius car with two seats. The original intention of manufacturing the car is not to compete with the existing ones, but to provide simple and practical small cars to the general public at a low price within the possible range. Those who purchase this car only need to pay a price of 100 pounds to get a car with two seats, and the fuel and recurring expenses are also very limited on weekdays. The Marius car factory has specially hired many car workers and greatly promoted its sales methods for the sake of manufacturing this new car.

▲ Chevrolet cars tour Germany Recently, a German company specializes in selling electric washing machines. They use Chevrolet trucks to tour the country as a promotional advertisement. The method is to use glass as the car body, with three washing machines inside. The motors of the car are used to show the working process. In addition to placing machines, there is still room in the car body for visitors to test on the spot. As a result, sales are booming. The company specially sent a letter to General Motors, praising the function of Chevrolet cars, saying that the journey was 14,000 kilometers and there were no obstacles along the way.

Book Review

Grassland Weekly, Fourth Volume, Numbers 4, 5, 6 186

In the transitional period of the gradual decline of proletarian literature and the deeper development of national literature, many nationalistic literary publications have emerged. Among these publications, "Grassland Weekly" is relatively strong and at the forefront. Although its format is small, its content is exceptionally brilliant and rich. It has now been published to the fourth volume. Artistically, it is clear that each issue has made great progress.

The recently published Fourth Volume, Numbers 4, 5, and 6, contains, in addition to the reporter's three "Post-Editorial Notes" and Wang Tiehua's "Waiting for You" and Huang Huanruo's "Consolation" (both continued), the following works: Mi Luo's "New Year's Blessing," "Fireside Chats," "Urban Loose Strings," Wang Fen's "Before and After Death," Guo Lanxin's "Steep Cliff," Tang Zengyi's "My Heart Burning Like a Coal," "Encouragement Song," "Miss Nina," Ye Du's "I Overlook from the Balcony," Hui Xiang's "Cuckoo in a Magpie's Nest," Wang Qihuai's "Liang Dingyuan," Zou Fang's "Three Pairs of Lovers," and "Literary News," etc., all of which are rare and valuable works.

Wang Fen's "Before and After Death" tells the story of a farmer named Chen Dabo's son. Since the son was clearly taken away by some army three or four years ago to serve as a soldier, he cursed soldiering and war. Later, his son suddenly returned home, but soon died of spitting blood. This was naturally due to wounds sustained in battle. The death of Chen Dabo's son made the people in the town deeply aware of the danger and terror of being a soldier. However, he instead received an inspiration from his son's last words. He thought:

"My son's fighting is revolution, revolution is glorious, and my son's death is also glorious. No one can avoid death. Rather than dying sickly in bed, it is better to take a bullet in the revolution, or die spitting blood like my son. When my son died, wasn't he not resentful? Perhaps he wasn't in pain. He himself said that serving as a soldier is what the people should do, revolution for the entire nation, and fighting for revolution is a good thing. Although he died, he was very happy because he said that he had fulfilled his duty as a citizen. So why should I worry and grieve?" Therefore, Chen Dabo did not hate war as he did in the past, and he explained to many young people who were afraid of being soldiers and encouraged them to participate in the revolution. After his death, several townspeople in military uniforms were already among those who came to mourn.

Self-interest and selfishness are common characteristics of the Chinese people, especially farmers with shallow knowledge. They have a deathly fear of being soldiers, and they do not care about the happiness of the entire population, but only fear the sacrifice of the small self. On the other hand, they selfishly feel that being a soldier is very easy. "Before and After Death," the author seized on this ideological mistake and gave them a major blow. In this way, we can know that the events expressed by the author in the work not only have a central consciousness of nationalism, but also give people a great inspiration. In terms of technique, the author also has a kind of power, this power is able to greatly excite our hearts. Just this "forceful emotion" can prove the author's success.

Wang Qihuai's "Liang Dingyuan" is also a very good creation. The author's description is very profound and moving. The story tells of an upward-looking young man who, seeing the current situation, "...with imperialism baring its fangs and claws, eager to try, and warlords and military men rampaging internally, killing and looting everywhere, so that natural and man-made disasters come frequently, causing the people of the whole country to cry out to the heavens, and corpses of the hungry are everywhere..." he felt "...we who live in this age of raging waves should have the spirit of striving upward. If I don't go to hell, who will? If I don't take this responsibility, who will take it..." So he resolved to follow Ban Dingyuan's story of giving up his pen and joining the army, leaving the university and entering military academy, to struggle for the survival and revitalization of the entire Chinese nation in a difficult environment.

After reading the outline of this novel, we can know how clearly our author recognizes the current era and the increasingly degraded national status. Therefore, the author awakens us, the youth who live in today's bitter age, that we should not hide behind the times, but must catch up with the tide of the times. The author further indicates the mission we should bear, "...We are young people, we must rise up and save ourselves, do not be pessimistic..." "Awaken national consciousness, unite our hearts and minds, and strive for the Chinese nation..." In the end, the author said so grandly, "...Father, let your current son Dingyuan shoulder this responsibility..."

This is indeed a powerful work of nationalist literature. As for the poetry in the three issues of "Grassland Weekly," Tang Zengyi's is the best. The author is a poet, and a poet with great talent. He also has a flood of fiery emotions, such as:

············

I hold up a precious sword,

To kill you, you violent one,

I wield a steel knife,

To kill you, you insidious one,

············

My heart burns like a coal

············

I am not afraid of the thorns everywhere,

Go, go bravely,

Cut off the obstacles of China,

Open up the barren Yai Mountain,

············

| Encouragement Song

These poems are full of passion and grandeur. How vigorously the author encourages us to strive for the Chinese nation. These poems all contain great significance and should be valued. It seems that too much has been said, so let's end here. The works introduced here are all relatively important. As for the rest, each article is limited by space and cannot be described in detail.
